[30;1m1408 | [0m[35m    Returns list of utf-8 byte and a corresponding list of unicode strings.[0m
[30;1m1409 | [0m[35m    The reversible bpe codes work on unicode strings.[0m
[30;1m1410 | [0m[35m    This means you need a large # of unicode characters in your vocab if you want to avoid UNKs.[0m

[30;1m1414 | [0m[35m    And avoids mapping to whitespace/control characters the bpe code barfs on.[0m

[30;1m924 | [0m[35m# - https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/64327[0m
[30;1m925 | [0m[35m# This allows us to de-shard without multiplying RAM usage, and also[0m
[30;1m926 | [0m[35m# conveniently drops the PyTorch dependency (though we still need numpy).[0m
